            "title": [
              ["${{ runner.os }}-${{ hashFiles('**/go.sum') }}", [["c"]]],
              [
                " tells when to clear the cache. In Go we want to do it when we change dependencies. Since the info about dependencies is stored in "
              ],
              ["go.sum", [["c"]]],
              [" file, we want to clear the cache if any of the "],
              ["go.sum", [["c"]]],
              [" files changes. This is done with "],
              ["${{ hashFiles('**/go.sum') }}", [["c"]]],
              [" which calculates a hash of all "],
              ["go.sum", [["c"]]],
              [
                " files. We don't want to re-use Windows cache on e.g. Linux (as they can differ due to build tags) so we add "
              ],
              ["${{ runner.os }}", [["c"]]],
              [" to the key name."]
            ]
          },
